Flight Simulator X, including X-Plane and the newest Lockheed Martin Prepar3D.\r\nFlightSim Logger works VERY WELL with every kind of aircrafts and helicopters included as built-in in the simulator or so on)\r\n- barometer adjustment (QNH, indicated in Hg)\r\n- simulation rate\r\n- flaps status\r\n- aircraft name\r\n- % throttle for each engines\r\n- gear status\r\n- autopilot master status\r\n- information here: https://developers.google.com/kml/).\r\nWith Google Earth data analysis, for example, you can see your flight in 3D mode, using all the data detected during the flight (latitude,
